Local News

Guangdong Representatives: Important Discussions Held Yesterday 146

Decision to Send Wu Chaoshu to Guangdong for Explanation

In addition to the Central Fourth Plenary Session, which concluded the day before yesterday, the Guangdong side currently has some opinions regarding the dual election issue in the seven preliminary peace conference resolutions, seemingly creating some setbacks for the future of peace. After the Central Government sent representatives such as Chen Mingshu to Shanghai for explanation, the situation became more optimistic. Guangdong representatives Wang Jingwei, Wu Chaoshu, Zou Lu, and representatives Ma Chaojun and Tan Zhen, who were sent to Shanghai by the Guangdong Fourth Plenary Session, convened a meeting at 6 PM last night to discuss remedial measures. The representatives deliberated until 7 PM before dispersing. According to Wang Jingwei, he and Mr. Hu Zhantang have decided not to return to Guangdong. Regarding this minor setback, in addition to immediately informing the Guangdong Extraordinary Conference by telegram, they also decided to send Mr. Wu Chaoshu, along with several military advisors from the Extraordinary Conference, back to Guangdong to report to the members of the Extraordinary Conference in person. The departure date of Wu and others has not yet been determined. Peace is not in jeopardy.

Wang Jingwei Issues Statement Yesterday 147

Regarding Guangzhou's Potential Veto of Peace Conference Resolutions

Yesterday's newspapers reported that the Fourth National Congress in Guangzhou on the 23rd had potentially vetoed the resolutions of the seven peace conferences. Guangdong representative Wang Jingwei issued the following statement to various news agencies yesterday: (Question) It is rumored that the Fourth National Congress in Guangzhou recently experienced setbacks in recognizing the resolutions of the peace conference. Is this true? (Wang's Answer) For several years, political disputes have unfortunately been resolved through military means. After Mr. Cai Ziming, Zhang Puquan, and Chen Zhenru arrived in Guangdong, I believed that a political solution was possible and devoted all my efforts to this. If the Guangzhou National Government's cancellation of the telegram and Mr. Jiang's resignation telegram could have been issued sooner, the setbacks could have been reduced. Although obstacles have inevitably arisen, I firmly believe that future disputes should be resolved through political methods and will continue to work hard, not disheartened by minor setbacks.

Wu Tiecheng Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday: Reports on Central Government's Hope 148

Special Foreign Affairs Committee Responds to Guangdong Representatives' Letter

Complete Agreement on Measures Regarding Japan

Requests Hu Jingwei and Others to Go to Beijing Immediately for Discussions

After the conclusion of the Fourth Plenary Session the day before yesterday, Central Committee member Wu Tiecheng took a train to Shanghai that night and arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning. He immediately visited the Guangdong representatives in Shanghai to discuss matters. It is reported that Wu's discussion concerned the opening of the Central Fourth Plenary Session and the election of the Fourth Central Committee members. In order to achieve unity within the party and unification of the country, the Central Fourth Plenary Session fully accepted the measures proposed by the Guangdong comrades at the Shanghai Preparatory Meeting. Wu also conveyed the Central Government's intention and hoped that the Guangdong Fourth Plenary Session would achieve a unanimous and satisfactory outcome. Regarding the Guangdong representatives Wang Jingwei, Wu Chaoshu, and Zou San's letter to the Central representatives on the 20th of this month regarding opinions on diplomatic relations with Japan, Wu also replied. The Central Special Foreign Affairs Committee entrusted Wu to reply to Wang and others as follows: Respectful regards to Mr. Wu Tiecheng. Mr. Cai Ziming forwarded the letter from Jingwei, Ti Yun, and Haibin, inquiring about three points. We have entrusted Mr. Cai Ziming to reply in detail to the three gentlemen. We are immensely grateful for the gentlemen's constant guidance. The current situation has become increasingly serious, and the Central Government is short-staffed and busy. Meetings are held daily from 7 AM to plan the day's response measures. After the meetings, telegrams are issued. The gentlemen should be well aware of this situation. Documents have accumulated to over a thousand pages. Our daily prayer is for the Guangdong comrades to come quickly to take charge. We have recently received a letter from the three gentlemen to Mr. Cai Ziming and others, the main point of which is that our country's representatives should invoke the precedent of Heep in the League of Nations Administrative Council and ask Briand to handle the Sino-Japanese incident using the same methods and means, and that treaty issues should not be discussed during this critical period. This is completely in agreement with the measures we have taken this time. Since the incident occurred, our country has appealed to the League of Nations based on the covenant because the League of Nations had previously resolved similar international disputes. Now that the matter is the same, the precedent can be followed. Ambassador Shi invoked the precedent at the Administrative Council meeting, and the Heep case was among them. We are now continuing to work hard to achieve the goals of preserving our country's territorial sovereignty and safeguarding international justice. However, what the members of the Central Government have consistently hoped for is that the gentlemen must come to Beijing quickly to discuss and handle the matter together. If this can be done, then there will be infinite benefits both externally and internally. The severity of the situation far exceeds the gentlemen's concerns. For the sake of the country and the party, we earnestly request that Mr. Zhantang, Jingwei, Ti Yun, Haibin, Zhesheng and others immediately come to Beijing. After arriving in Shanghai, please visit the gentlemen, explain everything here in detail, and do your best to persuade the gentlemen to prioritize the overall situation and come regardless. Because this kind of serious, urgent and troublesome situation can only be resolved through direct discussion. Being hundreds of miles apart, indirect communication through letters and telegrams means that we are already using the same claims and methods as those employed here. As for other important issues that must be discussed, it is not possible to consult frequently, which is very uneconomical. Not to mention the reduction in the unified strength of external affairs. Our sincerity is evident. Please convey this well and accept our best wishes. Respectfully, the Central Special Foreign Affairs Committee, Dai Chuanxian signed, November 23rd.

Various Sectors Urge Chiang to Go North 149

Cantonese Representatives Understand Issuance of Financial Bonds 150

Zhang Shouyong Says Total is 16 Million

75% Discount, Actually Receives 12 Million

According to a report from Huadong News Agency, concerning the Ministry of Finance's issuance of the 20th Year financial bonds, a senior official from the Ministry of Finance told a Huadong News Agency reporter yesterday that the Ministry of Finance, in light of the current national crisis, should drastically reduce all central military and administrative expenses. Therefore, all administrative expenses are issued at half the original amount, and military expenses have been reduced to 7.5 million per month. This, compared to the total national military expenses of 16 million per month for the central government, Northeast, and Shanxi, as determined in the previous Economic Conference, has already been reduced by more than half. However, even with various cuts, the annual budget still has a shortfall of more than 12 million. Hence, the proposal to issue financial bonds. The Cantonese representatives, due to a misunderstanding, sent a letter to the Shanghai banking community, urging them not to participate in the sale. However, after Minister Song met with Mr. Wang Jingwei a few days ago, they have already understood. In this critical time, the nation's finances should strive for stability. If an economic panic were to occur and lead to other changes, the consequences would be unimaginable. Both Nanjing and Guangzhou are eager for peaceful unification and are very sincere. They also express sympathy for stabilizing the nation's finances. Once explained, they all understood, so there is no problem with the issuance. At the same time, the people of the whole country should also understand that the Ministry of Finance repays approximately 15 million in principal and interest on foreign debt each month. Therefore, the issuance of this bond does not increase the original debt amount. As for the total amount of issuance, the banking community said it was 12 million. According to Vice Minister Zhang Shouyong of the Ministry of Finance, the total amount of issuance is 16 million. Because it is necessary to borrow from the banking community at a 75% discount, the actual amount received is 12 million. Hence, the misunderstanding of the total amount of issuance being 12 million. The original intention of the Ministry of Finance this time is completely in line with the unified financial committee plan produced during the peace conference.

From Today Until December 10th

The Shanghai Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association announced in its 18th public notice yesterday that the Japanese goods sealing survey form has been printed. Youth Automatic Northeast Anti-Japanese Corps Held Two Member General Meetings Yesterday 157

Sent Representatives to Meet Zhang Fakui

The details are as follows:

Two Member Meetings: At 1:00 PM yesterday, the corps held its second member general meeting in the meeting room on the second floor of the YMCA. 140 people attended. Zhang Shaojie chaired, and Zhu Dajun recorded. (1) Discuss the organization outline. Resolution: Establish four sections under the cadre meeting: general affairs, training, organization, and propaganda. The personnel for the positions will be decided at the next meeting. At the same time, request the Life Weekly to assist in raising the costs of future departures.

Zhang Fakui's Conversation: The corps sent representatives Zhang Shaojie and others yesterday to discuss with Mr. Zhang Fakui at his residence in Shanghai. (Q) When will you send troops to the Northeast? (A) Now that General Ma is isolated and helpless, and in imminent danger, it is imperative to send troops, but the date has not yet been decided. (Q) If the government does not allow you to go, what are your plans? (A) I firmly believe that the government will not prevent it. I am patriotic, but the procedures must be approved by the government. If it is not allowed, I will hand over the weapons to him and go empty-handed. I will die in the Northeast. (Q) Our comrades have now decided to go, and no matter what, they must go to the Northeast to assist. We are determined to use our blood to assist General Ma. We do not know what your intentions are. (A) Our patriotism is all sincere. I deeply admire the determination and enthusiasm of your comrades. In the current bad environment, it is admirable that you are gathering pure youth to sacrifice themselves to save the country. I am very grateful to you all. As comrades, I am willing to help. (Q) Our comrades are all empty-handed. Can you help with weapons? (A) We are all patriotic and killing the enemy. If I have weapons, I will do my best to provide them. (Q) Your praise for our comrades' actions is deeply ashamed. We do not know what your guidance is. (A) Your enthusiastic youth are automatically going to the Northeast to assist Ma in resisting Japan. All Chinese people should sympathize. However, you must coordinate funding, organize strictly, and maintain a stable position, proceeding according to your corps' purpose and plan. There will certainly be no problems. Finally, Mr. Zhang explained that the members of the corps are very pure, and their position is entirely for patriotism. Therefore, with the iron blood and to seek national survival, they are willing to shed blood first to awaken the general public. Whoever declares war on Japan will be the vanguard, and they have decided on the plan and steps to die. Commander Zhang was very sympathetic and hoped to work hard to fight to the end and added encouragement.

Mr. Zhang's Experiences 158

Regimental Commander Zhang Shaojie is a native of Hunan, currently thirty years old. He was formerly a student at Beijing Industrial University and worked at the Fengtian Aviation Office. He passed the examination for government-sponsored study of aviation in France. In the fifteenth year of the Northern Expedition, Mr. Zhang returned to China, participated in the Kuomintang's work, opposed the Eastern-Southern Expedition, and broke with the Feng faction. He served as the Dean of Education at the Guangxi Party Affairs School and as the Director of the Political Department of the Guangxi Anti-Communist Army General Headquarters.

Zhang Fakui Corrects Lu Fengshi's Remarks 160

Resisting Japan in the North is a Major National and Ethnic Affair

According to the Guowen News Agency, Zhang Fakui said yesterday that Mr. Lu Fengshi came to discuss the matter of resisting Japan. I did meet with him, and we only talked about my determination to resist Japan and that the route I planned to take was through Hunan and Hubei to Beiping, and then, depending on the situation, to coordinate with General Ma Zhanshan. Nothing else was discussed. However, after reading the report in various newspapers on November 24th, Lu Fengshi's published remarks by Zhang Fakui about the route of departure were not entirely truthful. The statements such as "[I would rather follow Chairman Jiang to proceed]," "[I believe I will receive a satisfactory response from both governments]," and "[I am willing to starve to death in Hunan]" are particularly shocking. A country can only have one government; this is an unchangeable principle. The struggle of the entire Fourth Army in the past few years and Fakui's personal stance are universally known and cannot be arbitrarily erased. Now that we are under the leadership of the revolutionary government produced by the Extraordinary Conference, we only know to act according to the revolutionary government produced by the Extraordinary Conference. Why is it necessary to obtain the consent and response of any other party? As for saying that we are willing to starve to death in Hunan without the government's assistance, it is even more absurd. The intention of Mr. Lu in writing these words is unknown. Resisting Japan is a major national and ethnic affair. How can the government and the people remain indifferent? Since there is a government and people as the backing for the anti-Japanese action, how can the anti-Japanese army starve to death?

Response to Zhang Fakui's Telegram

Letter from Guangdong Overseas Chinese Organizations 161

To Commander Zhang Fakui from the Executive Committee of the Guangdong Overseas Chinese Xin Shenghe Sports Association, Ju Zhao Xi Deng Shou and others: Commander Fakui, upon careful examination, since Jilin fell and Heilongjiang followed, anyone with a heart cannot help but feel pain. The Northeastern Army, once known for its雄霸, collapsed like a mountain at the first sign of foreign aggression. The blue sky and white sun are stained, and the reputation of the revolution is shamed. You, sir, are concerned about the peril of the country and have issued a telegram, causing both sadness and joy. With a call to arms, our rivers and mountains will shine. You are creating a precedent for national salvation among the military and inflicting pain on those who have lost our national territory. We dare to ask that you act on your words. Know that the invading Japanese have already occupied our territory for a long time, making the fortifications solid and difficult to recover. We humbly request that you quickly organize a strong army, depart early, drive the invaders out of the frontier, save our dying country, and rescue our people from under their iron hooves. Our association of more than eight hundred people is willing to be in the vanguard and swear to follow you to the death in the wilderness. We humbly ask for your consideration of our humble opinion and await your instructions. The entire eight hundred members of the Executive Committee of the Guangdong Overseas Chinese Xin Shenghe Sports Association bow.

A Collection of News About the Volunteer Army 167

The Second Regiment Headquarters of the Shanghai Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association Volunteer Army is currently located in the Haichang Public Office on Gonghe Xin Road in Zhabei. The following news was obtained from Regiment Commander Deng Jinglie.

Preparing for a Parade 168

Regiment Commander Deng, in order to make the people of Zhabei aware of the current national crisis and the need to mobilize the people to join the Volunteer Army, has decided to convene soldiers from the First, Second, and Third Battalions at the Qingyun Road open space on the 29th of this month for a parade through the streets. The route will roughly start from Qingce Road, pass through Xifuxing Road, Baoshan Road, the North Railway Station, the South Pier of the Han Bridge, Tianbaoli, Zhanjiang Road, Wuzhen Road, Guangfu Road, reach Datong Road at the Xinzha Bridge, Gonghe Road, Hengfeng Road, turn to Chang'an Road, and pass through the bustling streets of Gonghe Xin Road such as Qiujiang and Yongxingzhongxing to attract attention.

Field Exercises 169

The Third Battalion of the Second Regiment has been training at the Public Sports Ground in Nanshi with remarkable results. At 6:00 AM yesterday, they assembled at the ground again. First, Battalion Adjutant Ma Yiyong lectured on various marching scenarios. At about 7:00 AM, the officer on duty, Zhou Yongqi, along with company commanders Ying Caiwen and Wang Bin, led the departure. The vanguard was a military band formed by the battalion's soldiers, performing旅次 and marching songs. They indicated major rest and small rest stops during the march and pointed out the names of the terrain. At about 10:00 AM, they practiced at Caohejing, and then rested in the ancestral hall of Mr. Huang Jinrong. When Mr. Huang was inside, he sent people to rush to prepare drinks, etc. The soldiers then took out the biscuits and bread they brought with them to fill their stomachs. Then they bid farewell. It was heard that three soldiers from the regiment, Sun Baojian, had died a few days ago, and a mourning hall was set up at the Haichao Temple in Xiaonanmen. Therefore, they took a special route through Xujiahui into the French Concession to pay their respects. It was heard that the army marched the longest distance for the first time yesterday, about forty-odd miles, and they did not feel tired. There was also a female volunteer soldier among them. At the time of disbandment, she did not show any signs of fatigue, which was admirable.

Speech by the Director 170

The soldiers recruited by the regiment are all enthusiastic patriotic people from the local area. Therefore, in view of the recent loss of Heilongjiang Province, they are all heartbroken and ask Regiment Commander Deng to lead them to the Northeast to face the national crisis together. Commander Deng went to the Military Affairs Committee for this matter. The Deputy Director of the Training Department of the Military Affairs Committee was sent to the regiment the day before yesterday to give a speech, saying that at this time, he hoped that the soldiers would work hard to train in order to be used by the country. Regarding the matter of departure, the Military Affairs Committee is actively trying to proceed.

Strict Military Discipline 171

Hu Fengxiang, the Director of the Supervisory Department of the Military Affairs Committee, and Wang Changyuan, the Deputy Director, issued a notice for strict military discipline, saying: In order to issue a notice, it is known that this office has been formally established on November 10th and is specifically responsible for enforcing the law, special affairs, intelligence, and other functions. From now on, the military discipline will be strictly rectified. If there are any illegal officers or soldiers who violate the military discipline or engage in troublemaking outside, once found by this office or reported by others, they will be severely punished. This notice is hereby issued to all officers, soldiers, husbandmen, servants, etc. Be sure to comply with this notice.

The battalion headquarters of the Second and Third Battalions of the Second Regiment were originally located in the Chenxiangge inside the Xinbei Gate. Declaration of the Press Workers' Union 173

Aid to the Striking Workers of Datong Bookstore

The Shanghai Press Workers' Union's declaration to aid the striking workers of Datong Bookstore: Compatriots, hardworking brothers, the suffering of our working class needs no detailed explanation; everyone already knows it. Therefore, it is only natural and right for us workers to make demands on capitalists to improve our treatment, no matter when. The lives of us printing workers have always been very difficult, especially the bookstore workers. Their daily treatment is even worse than that of cattle and horses. Datong Bookstore, although it has strong capital, tall distribution offices, and wide factories, and can earn a lot of money every year, the capitalists of Datong Bookstore will never give the workers any treatment that is beneficial to them. Therefore, the strike of the workers of Datong Bookstore this time to demand conditions is an inevitable result. Their spirit is brave, their emotions are passionate, and all their demands can arouse our infinite sympathy, and we are willing to provide them with strong assistance. There are many people who say that we workers should not strike at this time of national crisis. This statement seems very right on the surface, but in reality, it is completely wrong. We workers understand very well that we should defeat imperialism and fight to protect national interests. At the same time, we also understand that we should improve our treatment and fight against capitalists to make demands. You can't act if you don't have food to eat. How can you participate in the anti-Japanese movement if you don't act? Therefore, participating in the anti-Japanese movement and the movement to improve treatment should go hand in hand. Those who oppose our workers' improvement of treatment under the pretext of Japanese imperialism's invasion are tantamount to starving us workers to death. Therefore, at this time of unrelenting foreign invasion, we should use all our strength to aid the struggle of Datong workers and oppose the capitalists of Datong Bookstore who oppress workers, and all kinds of evil forces. Compatriots, workers, everyone rise up! (1) Aid the workers of Datong Bookstore. (2) Oppose oppression of workers and improve workers' treatment. (3) Oppose oppression of the workers' movement and overthrow the labor traitors and lackeys. (4) Expand our workers' economic struggle and turn it into a revolutionary struggle against Japanese imperialism and against all domestic evil forces. Of course, this union respectfully leads all workers and will also strive and fight under these slogans. Shanghai Press Workers' Union.

Overview of German-Chinese Trade in the First Half of This Year 174

Imports Exceeding Exports by 41 Million Marks

After the European War, German-Chinese trade worked hard to develop, in order to restore the original state of the past. However, according to the statistics of the German financial authorities, in recent years, trade with China has still been importing exceeding exports. It is said that in the first half of this year, German-Chinese trade amounted to 71 million marks shipped by German ships to China, and 112 million marks shipped by Chinese ships to Germany, with imports exceeding exports by 41 million marks.

Local News Two

The Seven-Corpse Autopsy at Aiting Village 175

—Four Corpses Exhumed from Xiude Lane—

The Stench at the Time of Opening the Coffin Almost Made People Vomit

The Family Member Zhang Changgeng Claimed and Buried the Four Corpses

The Three Corpses Were Coffined and Buried by Personnel Sent by the Central Government

It Was Heard That Si Lie's Younger Brother Was Indeed Murdered

Seven corpses of family members of Gu Shunzhang, who were murdered by Communist Party members Zhou Enlai and others, were discovered in the underground of the front courtyard of the houses at numbers 33 and 37, Aiting Village, Yaozhujiao Road, in the French Concession. The corpses were four men and three women. They were temporarily coffined by the Shanghai Garrison Headquarters, marked with their names, and transported to the autopsy room of Tongren Fuyuan Branch for the autopsy. The details have already been reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now learned that those exhumed from number 37 were Gu Weizhen, Gu Wu's wife, Zhang Atao, and Zhang Aibao, a father and daughter. Those exhumed from number 33 were Wu Kechang and his wife, and the cook, Ma Pi, with no name. At 9:00 AM yesterday, the criminal section of the French General Inspectorate reported to the Second Special District Local Court for an autopsy. The Local Court reported to the Higher Third Branch Court and appointed Prosecutor Zhang Zongkan, along with Local Court Prosecutor Ding Shikui, forensic doctors Wei Ligong and Jiang Xuan, secretary Peng Yu, and bailiffs, to go to the site by car. When the autopsy was conducted, the family members and special commissioners of the Central Party Department had not yet arrived. The Shanghai Garrison Headquarters sent Yang Fengqi, the chief of the investigation team, to the scene to await instructions. The forensic doctors ordered the laborers to open the coffin lids one by one, and a stench filled the air, almost making people vomit. This autopsy was the first time that the autopsy room of Tongren Fuyuan Branch had encountered such a case. For the sake of hygiene, special rue, camphor, Dahurian angelica, atractylodes, sandalwood, and other fragrant items were prepared to be burned at the scene to slightly relieve the odor. The two forensic doctors, Wei and Jiang, each wearing rubber gloves, conducted a detailed examination of the corpses in the coffins. However, the coffin marked with Wu Kechang was found to contain a female corpse. It was not possible to identify the name, and it was mistakenly identified at the time of exhumation. In total, there were three men and four women. The hemp ropes around the necks of each corpse were cut off. They were wrapped in three to four or five to six strands, wrapped in paper, and marked with their names. The flesh of the corpses had not yet rotted, but their faces were blurred and unrecognizable. It was determined that each corpse had been strangled to death. After the examination, the prosecutor took the seat and first received a report from Yang Fengqi of the Shanghai Garrison Headquarters on the course of the case. Gu Jianzhong, a special commissioner of the Central Party Department, and Huang Kai, an employee of the Garrison Memorial Department, then arrived with Zhang Changgeng, a family member of the deceased. Zhang Changgeng testified that he was sixteen years old, a native of Shanghai, and that the deceased Zhang Atao and Zhang Aizi were his father and second sister. He identified them without error. The other corpses were all relatives of his brother-in-law, Gu Shunzhang, but he was not very familiar with them and it was now even more difficult to identify them. Gu Jianzhong, a special commissioner of the Central Party Department, stated that the names of the deceased were known based on the burial locations provided by the captured criminals. Prosecutor Zhang then recorded on the autopsy report that the deceased Zhang Atao, Zhang Aibao, Zhang Weizhen, and Gu Wu's wife had been identified by the family member Zhang Changgeng. Also, seven corpses, two female and one male, were all strangled to death. It was approved that Zhang Atao and the other four corpses could be claimed and buried by Zhang Changgeng. The three corpses whose names could not be identified would be taken into custody by Gu Jianzhong and Huang Kai, special commissioners of the Central Party Department, and the eight packages of hemp rope would be stored in the Local Court's stolen goods vault. After the autopsy, the prosecutor and others returned to the court to report the findings. The corpses were first prepared with clothing and bedding by the Garrison Headquarters, and then the laborers were ordered to re-coffin them and transport them to the Yanxu Villa (Tianxia Guild Hall) in Zhabei. It was also heard that there were originally rumors that nine corpses were buried in Aiting Village. Now that seven corpses have been exhumed, there may be omissions. Therefore, with the consent of the owner, Pan Zhaobang, numbers 34, 35, and 36 will continue to be excavated and inspected. In addition, four corpses were found yesterday morning in the small garden at number 6, Xiude Lane, Wuding Road, in the Public Concession, after the police sent people to excavate. The excavation time was around 9:30 in the morning. The district chief of the managing Gordon Road Police Station and Chief Inspector Krook also came to supervise the scene. At that time, there were many onlookers, no less than those on Yaozhujiao Road in the French Concession. About two hours after the excavation, a female corpse was discovered, and then more were discovered until a total of four corpses were unearthed. It was heard that the female corpse was the wife, mother-in-law, and female relative of something, and the male corpse was said to be the younger brother of Si Lie. Afterwards, they were all transported by car to the autopsy room to await today's autopsy.

A Trainee Was Shot Dead By a Guard Who Mishandled a Gun 176

His Head Was Shattered in a Tragic State

The District Chief and Patrol Officer Requested Punishment

At 10:15 PM the night before last, Liu Hongsheng, a guard at the 15th watch post of the Third District on the main street near Sanwanchang (place name) at the northern end of Huayuan Stone Bridge in Pudong, heard a commotion behind Sanwanchang. Guard Liu was deeply afraid that there would be an unexpected incident during this period of martial law. As a precaution, he first lifted the rifle he was carrying on his shoulder into his hands, loaded it with live ammunition, bent his waist, and walked with the gun held horizontally in front of him, intending to investigate the matter himself. Unexpectedly, the safety catch on the gun was not closed. The trigger was accidentally pulled, and with a bang, the bullet shot out. In fact, Jiang Xiaosizi (15 years old, from Jiangdu), an apprentice at the Yehua Iron Shop, was defecating by the small creek in front. The bullet went straight into Xiaosizi's back of the head and exited from his forehead, and he fell to the ground, covered in blood, and died on the spot. When the guard saw the cause of the disaster, he immediately returned to the district to surrender. The district chief questioned the guard and ordered him to be detained for further investigation. He then sent a message to the local police chief, Xie Along, to report to the Local Court for an autopsy. Afterwards, Jiang Fei's mother of the deceased lodged a complaint with the district, stating that her home was in the factory house of the Rihua Yarn Factory, that her husband had passed away many years ago, leaving behind four sons, and that the deceased was the youngest. It was unexpected that he would be shot and killed by the police gun. The guard had no feud with her son, so it was known that he did not fire the gun intentionally. She did not want to get involved in litigation. However, the family was poor and unable to afford to prepare a coffin. She asked the district chief what to do. The district chief took pity on her and gave her two hundred yuan from his own pocket to first pay for the coffin and funeral expenses and to take care of the funeral. At 4:00 PM yesterday afternoon, the Local Court appointed Prosecutor Zhao, along with attendants, to conduct an autopsy at the scene. It was found that the bullet exit point on the deceased's forehead was the size of a teacup, the brains were splattered, and the skull was shattered, and it was indeed the tragic state of being killed by a gunshot. No family members of the deceased were found at the scene. The corpse was ordered to be received and coffined by the owner of Yehua Iron Shop, Ye Zaihua, who signed a written pledge. It was heard that since this case occurred, although the family of the deceased had not filed a lawsuit according to the law, the police chief of the shed had not supervised them strictly, which led to this disaster. It was planned to ask the headquarters to demote him to police officer. The district chief and the patrol officer were negligent in training at ordinary times, so it was difficult to shirk responsibility. Therefore, he prepared a document and asked the headquarters to punish him. The shooting guard, Liu Hongsheng, was ordered to be sent to the headquarters and transferred to the court for strict investigation in accordance with the law.

<Correction of Candle Industry and Kerosene Wax Price P] In the recent city, a small number of candle industries only use kerosene to make candles, which is confusing with the price of tribute candles on the market. The Candle Industry Guild, in order to correct the price of the industry and to unify it, has separately discussed and decided to standardize and maintain business. The association specially notified all members yesterday, saying, "To whom it may concern, our association has recently had a small number of members who completely use kerosene wax to make candles, resulting in inconsistent prices, which is a hindrance to the business of most of the industry. At the general meeting on the 18th of this month, the candle was named kerosene wax, and from November 24th, each load will be sold at 30 yuan per load. The price of tribute candles and market candles will remain the same as before until new oil is seen, and there shall be no increase or decrease. In addition to sending letters to newspapers for announcements, we would like to solemnly inform you again, etc." Lihe Foreign Company Auctions Valuable Items. The proposals included: (1) Soliciting members to join the association; (2) The industry rules have been revised by the Social Bureau and investigators will be appointed. It was decided to appoint 11 people, Pan Yangsheng, Wang Zongcan, Zhong Gaosheng, Zhou Jisheng, Xue Deyi, Fang Changsheng, Liu Bingsheng, Shen Xinyu, Hu Shunmao, Shan Shaoting, and Yu Fuan, as industry rule investigators. They were not able to take office on the same day. (2) The association's operating expenses will be exempted from monthly donations from July 1, 2020. The Revenue and Expenditure Office will deduct one cent from each jar under the public sale item and allocate it to the association as operating expenses. (3) Methods for raising national salvation funds. In addition to the recognition of each member at that time, please ask each executive committee member to persuade each firm to save for emergency use. (4) Regarding the proposal to increase freight charges for Shaoxing wine transported from the gate to Shanghai, it was agreed to hand it over to the executive committee for discussion and handling. (5) The militia will be discussed and elected after the number of people is sufficient. The above were unanimously approved and the meeting adjourned. Cosmetics Industry. The Shanghai Municipal Fruit and Local Goods Industry Association sent a letter to the Committee for Implementing Economic Severance with Japan of the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday, saying, "To whom it may concern, I recently saw a report that Han Yuanchang Company's Korean apples produced in Korea were wholesale to Shanghai, etc., and attached a certificate from the Executive Committee of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, approving the sale. It is very strange to read it. After investigation, Korea is completely a Japanese colony. For example, the inspection team of our association had four baskets of apples shipped from Qingdao by Quanji Fruit Stall on the 20th of last month. After the review by our team, it was confirmed that the goods were Japanese goods. The Inspection Department of your association was immediately informed to seal up the goods and confiscate them for public use. As a result, these goods have since disappeared. Now the Korean apples transported and sold by Yuanchang Company are completely Japanese goods. Not only does our industry know, but other industries also know. It is really difficult to hide people's eyes and ears. In view of our association's enthusiasm for the Anti-Japanese War, we are specially writing to inform you. We hope that your association will handle it seriously and must be familiar with the identification of the goods to avoid confusion in the future of the Anti-Japanese War. The meeting was photographed and adjourned. Reader's Letter Inquiries from Mr. Wang Boming of Yixing (Ask about methods of resisting Japan and saving the country.) The cool moon shines on the ground, the sparse forest sways, and the north wind invades the bones, making people silent. Standing on the steps, I can't help but think of Jiangqiao in Heilongjiang Province, our loyal and brave soldiers, defending the country and resisting the enemy, and the bitter situation of melee and charge. The fallen soldiers and the soldiers who survived the war, facing this bright moonlight, were filled with grief and indignation, and wanted to eat the flesh of the Japanese. It can be imagined that at this critical moment of survival and death, who does not have the heart to destroy the Japanese and defend the country? However, everyone has their own responsibilities and cannot abandon their old business. They only hope that the Japanese invaders will realize their mistakes and withdraw their troops. However, thoughts are still thoughts, and facts are still facts. I am deeply concerned about the current situation, and my heart is increasingly pained. We were born as Chinese people, and we will die as Chinese ghosts. If the Japanese invaders destroy us, we will have no place to be buried. At this time, thinking about how to resist and how to fight is like whipping a dead horse. Therefore, I sincerely hope that before I die, I can do some practical things to save the country to repay my motherland. If I can fulfill my own ability and responsibility, I can leave a little regret in the world. However, Boming is a primary school teacher and cannot carry a gun to the front line to serve the country. As a man, I am ashamed and afraid. Every day, in addition to teaching children, I try my best to explain the atrocities of the Japanese army, instill common knowledge of resisting Japan and saving the country, and resolutely refrain from buying Japanese goods forever. I am deeply afraid that there are more important tasks of saving the country that can be done by millions of primary school teachers across the country, but we have not done them. How should we do them to be worthy of the armed patriotic men in the icy and snowy trenches? May I ask you, sir, what else do we need to do? (Reply) Primary school teachers, speaking from their own profession, are already extremely important. For example, General Ma Zhanshan, who is universally admired by the compatriots across the country, gentlemen in the education circle, should at least study the following two questions: (1) What kind of education did Ma Zhanshan receive to have this kind of thinking and action? (2) Is the current education sufficient to cultivate people like Ma Zhanshan? If the results of the research show that the current education is not enough to cultivate them, or even enough to cultivate non-resistant generals who are absolutely opposed to Ma Zhanshan, what is the benefit of this kind of education to the future of the country and the nation? This is one of the tasks that educators should have because of this national crisis. As for explaining the actions of the Japanese army, instilling common sense of saving the country, and always buying enemy goods, if the education circle issues a mobilization order, primary school teachers across the country will all vigorously implement these three tasks, and they will never be allowed to relax until a demobilization order is issued. How great, solid, and long-lasting will the future effect be? These are all things that the education circle should and can do. I would like to ask if there are other things to do. Ms. Huang Huibai of Suzhou sent six articles of the national salvation oath. We think they are very important and should be observed by all compatriots. All educators should universally teach young people and set an example themselves, which is their unshirkable responsibility. Ms. Huang Huibai's letter (I hope that the people of the country will practice the six articles of the national salvation oath.) The way to save the country lies in vigorous practice. I respectfully order six old agreements and hope that the people of the country will abide by them and persevere throughout their lives. (1) From today onwards, I vow to stop all entertainment banquets and miscellaneous consumption (such as drinking alcohol, sipping tea, and smoking cigarettes) and transfer the money saved to the national salvation fund. (2) From today onwards, I vow to practice frugality in clothing and food, and to fulfill the doctrine of thrift, and transfer the expenses saved to the national salvation fund. (3) From today onwards, I vow to practice physical education for one hour every day and read books that are beneficial to the body and mind for one hour. (4) From today onwards, I vow to work harder on my original work. (5) From today onwards, I vow not to use enemy goods and not to use foreign goods unless absolutely necessary. (6) From today onwards, I vow to persuade at least one person every day to implement the above oath. Reading Dr. Wang Yuanchen's Judgment Admonition (Liu Wushu) Yi Ruichang sought treatment at the Jiangsu Provincial Hospital due to the inability to move his C-joint joint. Dr. Wang Yuanchen, the director of the hospital, administered acupuncture and medicine, and the ulceration was greatly healed. The patient wanted to save and treat the joint adhesion of the femoral joint in the hope that the disabled limb could recover its movement. Dr. Wang told him that the syphilis was deep, the stiffness was long-lasting, and it was difficult to cure. If it must be cured, there are only two methods: surgery and shaking. He also stated the danger of fracture with shaking. In desperation, the patient wanted to seek a chance of hope and tried his best to save the surgery, and used [dead horse as a live horse doctor] as a metaphor. (The patient did not want surgery, so he took the shaking method.) Dr. Wang can be said to have avoided difficulties and enthusiastically performed his duties. Unexpectedly, shaking the right femur had already shown results, and then shaking the left femur, because the syphilis was deep and the bone quality was brittle, the bone was broken before the surgery was completed. Wang then transported it to the Hongren Hospital and joined it under the X-ray light. The surgery that could be applied had been used, and the doctor had done everything he could, and he could plead not guilty to the patient's family. Nai Yi Ruichang, after eight or nine months, was heavily indebted (owed more than 800 yuan in medical expenses) and his disability had not healed. He had a wonderful idea and accused Director Wang of negligence in business, resulting in serious injury, in the court. The Zhenjiang Local Court had a unique eye and charged Director Wang with negligence in business, resulting in serious injury. I read it with emotion. The guilt or innocence of Director Wang can be decided in one word, that is, whether Yi Zaichang's serious injury (referring to the inability to move the joint) was caused by Director Wang. If this doubt is cleared, the rest can be easily solved without the need for words. People with little common sense of medicine may suspect that the broken thigh bone is an incurable matter. I don't know that patients with tertiary syphilis have the possibility of fracture with this surgery. However, if it is unfortunately broken, it can also be connected. If the interface is not neat, it is just unsightly in appearance. At most, the action is weak. There is no reason why the joint cannot move due to the fracture at three inches below the great trochanter, nor is there any reason why the joint becomes stiff if the interface is not very neat. This can be known by those who have a little common sense of physiology, without the need for medical experts. Last year, there was someone who sought treatment from me for a feverish disease. The radius was fractured for a long time, and the shoulder joint and elbow joint moved freely. The broken limbs and tibias of disabled soldiers are everywhere, and the joints above the broken end are intact. Knowing this, Yi Ruichang's disability is due to many years of syphilis, which makes the joint adhere and unable to move. At first, it has nothing to do with whether the bone is broken or not, and it has nothing to do with the neatness of the bone connection. Since the serious injury was not caused by Director Wang, what is the negligence in business? The root of this charge cannot be established. First, this case has been handed over to experts for appraisal twice, and it is quite fair. Since the judgment is cited as the basis, it cannot harm the meaning with words and lose its original intention. Nai judge took the part of the appraisal report that was beneficial to the plaintiff out of context and adopted it into the judgment. Other fair and detailed parts that were beneficial to the defendant were not only implicitly ignored, but also did not hesitate to contradict them, and stubbornly pretended to know what he did not know, and concocted the crime, saying that [after the treatment, because the thigh bone was shaken and reconnected, after a long period of time, the poisonous bacteria gathered between the hip and knee joints, resulting in strong fixation and inability to move slightly. With the intervention of this natural cause, the defendant's criminal responsibility cannot be interrupted, and he must be held responsible for negligence in business, resulting in serious injury]. I don't know where this wonderful theory comes from. Why does the gathering of germs in the hip and knee joints result from the thigh bone being shaken and reconnected after a long period of time? If this is the case, is the inability to move the two hip joints before the surgery (Yi Ruichang's own complaint and statement to the appraiser) caused by shaking and reconnecting the thigh bone? Is the inability to move the right joint Director Wang's fault? It is far-fetched to impose a crime on others. Then, all surgeries with dangerousness, if the result is bad, can be concocted into a prison. Who dares to be a doctor? It is said that in case of doubt about a crime, be lenient; in case of doubt about merit, be generous. Why are the ancients and modern people so contradictory? Moreover, I have more questions that I don't understand. Director Wang's defense statement should not be lightly believed by the judge, which is appropriate. The points clearly proven in the plaintiff's own complaint and the appraisal report are also not paid attention to. This is what we, the common people, cannot understand after thinking about it a hundred times. I will enumerate a few items to prove it. (To be continued) 177

Automotive News Special Article A General Overview of Next Year's New Cars. Song. Styles and Structures Have Improved. The year 1932 will soon be here. There will be a new atmosphere in the automotive market. This is the best time to introduce new cars at the end of the year. Therefore, a summary of the styles of next year's new cars and the differences from the current models is given below. Regarding the style and structure of the chassis, except for a few that have been reformed, most are the same as the 1931 models. All the places that need to be reformed are derived from experience. As for the size and style of the body, according to Mr. Gan Liss, current automotive operators, in view of the national and international situation, most car buyers tend to favor small cars because they are cheaper to buy and are extremely economical to use in peacetime. Therefore, there will be a large number of small cars on the market in the future. Therefore, manufacturers are now focusing on four-cylinder and twelve-horsepower small cars. This is also due to the fashion of buyers. The structure and style of the body have always been changing with each passing day. Therefore, it is expected that there will be many styles of new car bodies next year. Anyone who sees this kind of new car will initially think that it is roughly the same as the current style. However, after careful observation, it will be found that there are many reforms. Generally speaking, the excellent body of the new car is that it is spacious, wide and deep, and its front part is also more comfortable. This point may not be visible at first glance, but those who are in the car will definitely feel it. The body of the new car is lower than the old one. This is because the chassis is low, so the body is also low. In addition, or because the configuration of each part of the car is even, it also feels low and beautiful. Therefore, the car line is also mostly changed. Although it is not most of it, it is also very careful. Moreover, not only the majority of the body's panels are curved, but also the wings are all the same. This is because flat steel is used more and more in car manufacturing. Not only the all-steel body is like this, but the wooden frame of the assembled body is also inlaid with flat steel. The appearance style of the car is the most important issue in the current car manufacturing industry. The smooth or sluggish car sales mostly depend on the quality of its style. Therefore, next year's new car will spend a lot of research and effort on the style issue. However, this does not mean that the car's action shape can be ignored. Generally speaking, car drivers with special identification ability pay great attention to the car's action shape. However, this point is best if it can match the car's identity. However, car manufacturers must pay great attention to the style, appearance, and after-sales service of a well-made car, because this often attracts the choice of those who intend to buy a car. For this reason, the style of the new car is a major focus of car manufacturers. Not only is the side view emphasized, but also the front shape and the back view are taken into account. In terms of the above-mentioned scope, the radiator, high beam lamps, and horns on the car must be taken into account in all aspects. Their installation is often made to match the whole car. In the past, car manufacturers often had a style in mind for the construction of the radiator. They often did not consider whether it was in harmony with the whole car. When it was completed, the style was not unattractive, but often the driver's line of sight was obscured by this radiator. When manufacturing the rear part of the car, attention was also paid to its style. Generally speaking, the trend is to be a whole piece. The spring hook chain is of course made in an extended style. At present, the construction of various cars, spring hook chains, and metal rings are mostly lubricated in a centralized manner, so in fact, there is no need to expose the various parts to the outside. The brake adjuster and shock absorber devices are largely the same as before. An important feature of next year's new cars in terms of style is that the chassis and the body are properly configured, the size is uniform, and the form becomes a whole harmony, not a clear division into two sections. The sides of the body are very deep, so that the curtains can be avoided. This trend is very popular now. The new car will also adopt it. However, the running board, which was once wanted to be eliminated, is still retained, because this kind of equipment can help the wings to protect against mud. It is very necessary in rainy days. Even if the car uses tight wings, this kind of short running board must be adopted. The reason is as mentioned above. A style adopted by the famous lawyer Ma and the Rover cars is also worth noting, that is, the front part is flat or army style. This kind of style can only be seen in custom-made cars in the past, but recently it has been chosen by various standard cars, which is also worth mentioning. As for whether this kind of style is an improvement, this should be viewed from the whole car as a whole. However, it is a fact that it can make the inside of the car brighter. In fact, for this kind of car head, the driver often wants to install a wind screen to avoid the glare. If this kind of device is needed, it should not be an outer cover style, otherwise the style will be affected. The panel of the sunshade is attached to the top of the car when not in use. It is very convenient to use this simple method with just one hand. Although the windshield is a small matter, it is worth mentioning here. At present, the trend is to adopt a fixed windshield. Once installed, it cannot be opened arbitrarily. In fact, even in extremely hot weather, there is no need to open the windshield. However, there is one thing that is very inconvenient for fixed windshields, that is, foggy days and when the temperature drops. At that time, the fog is misty and adheres to the windshield and becomes moisture. Even if there is a water scraper, it is useless. Fortunately, this kind of weather is very rare. Buyers of cars with fixed windshields do not have to worry too much. Cars with four doors are very convenient for users, which is undoubtedly. In the new cars of next year, there will be many styles of two-door two-seater cars. This kind of vehicle is actually for two people, but there are also other devices that can seat four people. Most of the sedan cars that can carry four or five people are equipped with four doors for convenience. The new cars of 1932 will have great improvements in color, bright and pleasing to the eye. The range of all kinds of colors is very wide, which is very different from the past when there were only a few kinds of colors and black was preferred. The use of wood material with glossy paint is very popular. Car manufacturers have made great contributions to this point. Compared with one or two years ago, it is much more beautiful. Even in low-priced bodies, the glossy materials used in the color aspect can now be comparable to custom-made cars. If this kind of glossy paint is used properly, it is also very durable. Since the above-mentioned wood material with glossy paint is used, the color of the body is renewed and dazzling. The fabric material of the body is no longer liked by people. Today, although there are still many people who like the fabric material of the body, if you want it to be bright and durable, you must spend a lot of effort on protection, otherwise it will look old in two years. There is also an aspect of the body manufacturing in 1932 that is very important, that is, car merchants have opened up a new way in their business policies. That is, some chassis manufacturers will unite with manufacturers that specialize in making exquisite carriages, so that the cars produced under this kind of cooperation will become a kind of (standard special body). This name seems very special at first glance, but in fact, this kind of body is manufactured firmly and the materials are excellent, which is worth the price. The cars produced by the cooperation between manufacturers and body manufacturers will be welcomed by customers who generally like novelty and curiosity. If the body manufacturer does not cooperate with the manufacturer, then the manufacturer has no other way to think of except for manufacturing a standard car. This can also be said in reverse, that is, the demand for standard cars is high, and the demand for standard special cars is rare. Qu Chengqing: Bandits Sentenced to Death 178

Bao Lao Er Imprisoned for Seventeen Years

Qu Chengqing, residing at No. 1760 Haining Road, was kidnapped by bandits on January 11th of last year at 11 PM, just as he returned home and reached his doorstep. The two perpetrators, Shi Arong from Ningbo and Bao Lao Er (also known as Rongqing) from Taizhou, were apprehended by the combined efforts of the Huishan and Huisi police stations. They were handed over to the First Special Court. After repeated interrogations, the trial concluded yesterday at 2:30 PM. Presiding Judge Wu Tingqi announced the verdict in the Second Criminal Court. The main points were as follows: Shi Arong was sentenced to death for the crime of jointly kidnapping for ransom; Bao Lao Er was sentenced to seventeen years of imprisonment with hard labor for the crime of jointly kidnapping for ransom, with two days of pre-trial detention counting as one day of imprisonment.

Wei Tingrong Kidnapping Case: Zhao Weisheng's Identity Question 179

Ministry of Justice Certifies Zhao as a Military Man

Final Arguments Concluded, Sentencing Scheduled

In the kidnapping case of Wei Tingrong, former Commander-in-Chief of the French Concession Chinese Volunteer Corps, which occurred in July of the eighteenth year of the Republic, the French police apprehended Zhu Jingcheng, Chen Zhongheng, and Tang Shiliang, who were then handed over to the French court. They were tried and sentenced, as recorded in the case files. Subsequently, the French police apprehended other involved parties, including Lü Ruowang, Cai Weicai, and Zhao Weisheng, who were handed over to the Second Special District Local Court and held in custody. Yesterday at 3 PM, Judge Xiong Huiben, along with court clerk Tao Zongkan and Prosecutor Lou Guanguang, convened in the First Court for the hearing. The defendants were represented by lawyers Zhu Dianqing, Gao Wenqi, Shan Yuhua, and Ge Zhaoji. First, Zhao Weisheng's defense lawyer, Mr. Shan, stated that the court had previously requested an interpretation from the Ministry of Justice regarding the defendant Zhao Weisheng's identity. It has now been verified that Zhao is indeed a military officer. Concerning the issue of jurisdiction, he requested that Article 318, Clause 6 of the Criminal Procedure Law be addressed first. The court instructed that the trial proceed, and Zhao was then questioned, stating that he was 31 years old, from Zhengzhou, Henan, and currently serving as the commander of the Sixth Independent Battalion of the Ministry of Finance's Tax Police. He was further questioned about the battalion's organization, jurisdiction, and duties. Lü Ruowang testified that he did not know about the kidnapping of Wei beforehand. He met Zhou Juying and Chen Chuheng at a fair in Hangzhou. Zhou gave him a letter and a form, instructing him to go to the Chengzhan Hotel to collect 1,000 yuan. Later, upon returning to Shanghai, he met Zhao Weisheng on the roof of the Wing On Department Store, who spoke about the kidnapping of Wei. Cai Weicai testified that Yang Ada, Fan Rengen, Xu Liyuan, and Zhang Agen went to carry out the kidnapping. He was instructed to watch the north side of Avenue Edward VII for foreigners. Initially, they said they were going to rob opium, but he later learned about the kidnapping of Wei. At this point, the court ordered Zhu Jingcheng, Chen Zhongheng, and Tang Shiliang, who had already been sentenced, to be brought in for cross-examination. Zhu and Tang both stated that they did not know about the kidnapping of Wei and that their previous confessions were coerced. Chen Zhongheng testified that Lü first introduced Zhou Juying, who borrowed 1,200 yuan from him, claiming it was to open a printing shop. Later, because the money was not repaid when due, Zhou arranged a meeting with Zhao Weisheng on the roof of the Wing On Department Store. Zhao told him that Wei was wealthy but unkind and had embezzled public funds from the Volunteer Corps. He wanted to kidnap him and said that the money Zhou borrowed was not for opening a printing shop but for the kidnapping. Later, he went to Hangzhou to see the fair and met Lü and Zhou on the road. The next afternoon, Lü Ruowang and Zhou Juying went to his house. Zhou said the 1,000 yuan was borrowed at the Chengzhan Hotel and instructed him and Lü to go collect the money. Zhou handed over a letter. He was anxious to get the money, so he went with Lü. Upon arriving at the Chengzhan Hotel, he overheard Lü negotiating with someone in the room and realized it was about the kidnapping of Wei. He panicked and fled, but Zhou Juying grabbed him, threatened him with a pistol, and dragged him back into the room. Zhao Weisheng firmly denied knowing Lü Ruowang and Chen Zhongheng and denied meeting and discussing the kidnapping of Wei on the roof of the Wing On Department Store. At this point, the court ordered the commencement of closing arguments. After the defendants' lawyers presented their defenses, the police lawyer Fei Xizhen gave a detailed argument on the defendants' criminal conduct. The court adjourned the arguments and scheduled sentencing for the morning of November 18th. The defendants were remanded into custody. During the hearing, Zhao's family and subordinate military officers were present in the audience. By the time the court adjourned, the clock had struck five.

Zhihe Qianzhuang Case Hearing Held Yesterday 180

The case of accountant Tang Zaizhang, the court-appointed liquidator, suing the shareholders of Zhihe Yongji Qianzhuang was heard by Judge Li Mo in the Ninth Court yesterday morning at 9 AM. First, the plaintiff, accountant Tang Zaizhang, presented his audit findings, stating that he had submitted a detailed table of assets and liabilities to the court, showing what the company owed and what was owed to it. While the amounts owed to and by the company appeared to balance on the surface, in reality, there was no hope of recovering the 1.2 million taels owed by Shen Chengji alone, and there were many other bad debts. Since his appointment, he had only received 70,000 to 80,000 taels, which were temporarily deposited in a bank, awaiting distribution. Lawsuits were being pursued against the remaining debtors, but it was difficult to expect recovery in the short term. There were over 400 depositors, mostly small creditors. To protect these creditors, it was necessary for the shareholders to step forward and settle the matter. Furthermore, when the liquidator collected debts for the qianzhuang, debtors often requested reductions in the amount owed. Although this was clearly permitted by facts or reason, because the shareholders were avoiding involvement, the liquidator could not grant these requests, making the liquidation process increasingly difficult and causing even greater losses for the general creditors. Therefore, he urged the shareholders to come forward and settle the matter as soon as possible. He then listed the names of the shareholders, stating that the shareholder register and capital book contained detailed information and were sealed with a continuous stamp, providing solid evidence. Lawyers Wang Youling and Li Xinyang, representing the plaintiff, presented their legal arguments. The defendant Chen Yizhai retained lawyers Zhang Zhirang and Wang Fusheng, while the defendant Chen Rongrongchu retained lawyer Zhang Zhengxue. They took turns responding and requested further collection of evidence. Lawyer Xu Shihao, representing the creditors, requested that the shareholders' assets be provisionally seized. The judge summarized the facts and arguments and announced that the hearing would be adjourned and reconvened. All shareholder cases would be consolidated and heard together. Regarding the request for provisional seizure, he instructed that a formal application be submitted for further review.

Firecracker Explosions Cause Injuries 181

Two Injured in Loud Blast

Shen Yugan, from Jiangbei, opened a firecracker (small firecrackers bought by children for playful throwing) workshop last year in a flat at No. 5, Lane 79, Yangjiazhai, Pudong. He employed over ten female workers, and production was quite fast. However, in addition to sand and gravel, these firecrackers required gunpowder. Yesterday at 9:15 AM, Shen was mixing the gunpowder when, due to carelessness, an explosion suddenly occurred. The loud blast shook the surrounding area. The loft of the workshop was blown apart, and the walls of two houses collapsed. Shen himself was directly hit by the blast, suffering severe facial injuries. His face was swollen and disfigured, resembling a drowned corpse. His clothes were torn to shreds, and he collapsed to the ground, unable to move. A young female worker, Yang Xiaoju, only twelve years old, had a large hole blown in her right eye, with blood gushing out. Residents nearby, hearing the loud explosion, were initially unsure of what had happened and were greatly alarmed. Nearby police officers sent men to transport the two injured individuals to the Third District, from where they were transferred to Pudong Hospital for treatment. It is reported that Shen's injuries are not life-threatening, but he may lose his sight. The Third District Chief, Zhang, ordered all unexploded gunpowder to be removed from the area after the incident. It was also discovered that there were five such firecracker workshops near Yangjiazhai. In addition to instructing them to cease operations, he also submitted a request to the General Bureau to prohibit all firecracker workshops in the city from operating to eliminate the danger.

The Development of the Chihchih Savings Society 182

The Chihchih Savings Society was founded in the city by postal workers in the 18th year of the Republic. Over the years, it has developed considerably. Previously, the society was instructed by the Bureau of Social Affairs to increase its capital to prevent abuses. The society has already raised funds to reach 10,000 yuan. It is reported that after the society distributes its second dividend next month, it will begin offering small credit loans on January 1st of next year to address the legitimate urgent needs of the public.

A Man Assassinated 183

At around 9 AM yesterday morning, a man wearing a dark blue serge robe and a melon-shaped hat was walking in the Zhangjiazhai area of Carter Road when he was suddenly attacked by an assailant who opened fire. Three shots were fired, hitting the man in the back of the head and left waist. The man collapsed to the ground due to his severe injuries and died on the spot. A police vehicle took the body to the morgue for examination. The deceased was approximately thirty years old.

Record of the National Endeavor Society Preparatory Meeting 184

The National Endeavor Society held a preparatory meeting at the YMCA on North Sichuan Road yesterday afternoon at 4 PM. Attendees included Huang Jingwan, Xu Wancheng, Wu Ziqian, Liu Suijiu, Miao Zhijie, Cheng Zuxin, Xia Chao Fan, Ms. Zhou Wenji, and observers, totaling over 300 people. Wu Ziqian chaired the meeting, and Xu Wancheng took minutes. After the formalities, the chairman reported on the purpose of the meeting, followed by an introduction of Professor Liu Suijiu of Northeastern University, who spoke on Japan's past conspiracies and current atrocities in the three northeastern provinces. Those who heard him were filled with righteous indignation. The following matters were discussed: (1) Establish a national general association first, and then set up branches in various provinces to facilitate operations. (2) Notify representatives from various locations to register promptly so that the general assembly can be held as scheduled. (3) Set up a reception center at No. 120, Dachongli, Tongfu Road. (4) Decide to hold the inaugural meeting at 2 PM on the 29th of this month in the auditorium of the YMCA. (5) Appoint Liu Suijiu as chairman of the general assembly, Ms. Zhou Wenji as master of ceremonies, Xu Wancheng as the recorder, and Miao Zhijie and Xia Chaofan to arrange the venue and reception for the general assembly. (6) Wu Ziqian, Cheng Zuxin, and Huang Jingwan were appointed to handle the reception of representatives from various provinces. (7) Review the applications of new members submitted on the spot. Over eighty qualified applicants were approved for registration. The matter of requesting the society's constitution from other cities was not resolved. Requests from outside the province should be directed to the reception center for representatives from other provinces, and requests within the city should be made to Mr. Miao Zhijie at the YMCA.

Large Quantities of Silver Dollars Shipped to Dalian 185

Amounts Reaching Over Six Million

From the middle of this month to the present, the market price of Dalian silver dollars has been unusually high, equivalent to 7 qian, 7 fen, and 6.7 li per Shanghai tael. According to market prices in both locations, a profit of over 500 taels can be made for every 10,000 yuan. Therefore, banks, qianzhuang, and merchant guilds have been actively shipping silver dollars, totaling over six million. The shipments are being handled by the Dongshunji and Nanrongji customs brokers. It is also reported that further shipments are expected in the next few days. However, with the current rampant violence of the Japanese, shipping large quantities of silver dollars to Dalian to support their aggression is a suicidal policy for Chinese merchants who are greedy for small profits and forget the greater harm.

Notice to Those Aspiring to Study in England 186

The Continental Press reports that the Chinese Committee of British Universities has established an office to facilitate the affairs of Chinese students who aspire to study in England and those already studying there. Mr. B. Endeligh has been appointed as honorary secretary. His address is Street London W.C.L. Mr. Xue will cooperate with the Chinese Consul-General in England. Any inquiries regarding accommodation, education, introductions to factories, university admission procedures, etc., whether made by letter or in person, will be answered free of charge.

First Phase: American Relief Wheat Shipped to China 187

Thirty-Two Ships to Arrive Within Three Months

Totaling Over 189,000 Tons

The relief wheat purchased from the United States has already been shipped to China in three vessels, heading to various ports along the Yangtze River, totaling over 26,000 tons. The Fook Lai Shipping Company, which is transporting the wheat, has received a telegram from the United States stating that the first phase of shipping relief wheat to China will run from October 9th (when the first batch of wheat was shipped from the United States and is expected to arrive in Shanghai on the 17th of this month) to December 29th. A total of 32 ships will be used, with 22 ships scheduled to unload in Shanghai and the remaining 10 ships scheduled to unload in Nanjing, Jiujiang, and Hankou. The wheat unloaded in Shanghai will be transferred to Changjiang Company ships and transported to Hunan, Hubei, Anhui, and Jiangxi. The Relief Disaster Relief Office has negotiated with various shipping companies for a freight rate of 4 taels and 2 qian per ton from Shanghai to Hankou. Of these 32 ships, the total amount of wheat designated for transport is 133,591 tons, and there are also 55,951 tons of flour, totaling 189,541 tons, approximately 3,184,308 dan, valued at approximately 16.7 million national currency. In addition to the four ships that have already arrived, there are also 6,720 tons of wheat and 1,298 tons of flour on the Vancouver City, which left the United States on October 27th and is expected to pass Wusong today. This cargo is destined for Hankou. Another vessel, the Victoria City, is carrying 6,650 tons of wheat and 1,505 tons of flour, which left the United States on the 6th of this month and is expected to arrive in Jiujiang on December 3rd for unloading. These two ships carrying relief wheat are insured for 640,000 US dollars. The first phase of cargo is expected to be fully loaded and arrive in Shanghai by the end of January. The remaining 260,000 tons are scheduled to be loaded starting in January of next year. The first ship of the second phase is the Willindon Card, carrying 7,800 tons of wheat and 1,100 tons of flour, destined for Shanghai. The details of the ships designated to load the first phase are listed below:
