Shipping News

Chinese Merchants Eagerly Purchase New Ships 188

Since the outbreak of the Anti-Japanese War, Japanese ships in China have had no business whatsoever. Chinese merchant ships have recently been very crowded on all routes along the rivers and seas, with a clear excess of cargo over available ships. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has already purchased two ocean-going vessels and ordered two 700-ton riverboats from the Dahua Shipyard to expand its shipping operations on the Southern and Upper Yangtze lines. The Sanbei Company has also purchased three ocean-going vessels from Hong Kong, the largest of which is 6,000 tons. It has already assigned employees to go to Hong Kong to take delivery of the ships and bring them to Shanghai. It is said that the remaining two ships are former ocean-going vessels of a British trading company in Shanghai, which Sanbei will repair and then schedule for routes.

Jiangshun Searches for Armed Drama Troupe 189

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Jiangshun vessel, on its voyage from Hankou to Shanghai, carried 500 new recruits and a propaganda team of 50-60 members. At 6 AM on the 19th, while en route from Wuxue, and just as it was about to check passenger tickets in Jiujiang, a conflict arose between the new recruits and the propaganda team over hot water. Personnel in the refugee quarters witnessed the situation and attempted to mediate. However, the members of the propaganda team were impatient and aggressive. The ticket inspector Zhang Gensheng immediately notified the on-board military police to come and mediate, hoping to resolve the matter. Unexpectedly, the team members misunderstood, thinking that Zhang Gensheng was relying on the military police to suppress them. They then encircled Zhang and blew a whistle to call for help. Although the military police mediated, Zhang Gensheng was still seized by the team members, who accused him of insulting their team leader and demanded that he be severely punished as a warning. Zhang, to protect himself, claimed to be a tea server, and Inspector You verified that he was indeed a tea server. The propaganda team then forced Zhang to the ground and gave him sixty heavy strokes of the cane. It is unknown whether the incident was fully resolved.

Pusong District Affairs Meeting 190

The Pusong District Municipal Committee Office held its 13th district affairs meeting the day before yesterday (23rd) at 1 PM. The meeting was chaired by Chen Ya Fu. After the formalities, the chairman reported on: (1) repairing streets and bridges in various towns; (2) adding garbage cans in various towns; (3) planning the dredging of river ports and construction of roads; (4) disaster relief for 30% of the forced labor tax in the drought; and (5) preparing for self-government. Resolutions: 1. Previous resolutions to dredge rivers and waterways in various locations should be compiled and urgently requested from the Municipal Government for dredging. 2. Rent reduction for tenant farmers should be considered as much as possible before the Land Bureau issues an official order. 3. A letter should be sent to the District Planning Committee to add five investigators according to the allocation of investigators in each district. 4. A letter should be sent to the Public Security District Office and various district and local police chiefs to assist in preparing for self-government. Other temporary motions were discussed, and the meeting was adjourned.

Deng Fenweng Calligraphy and Engraving Exhibition 191

Deng Fenweng, a famous calligrapher and engraver in Shanghai, will soon display his 130+ new works, along with some works of social commentary, all finely mounted, from the 27th of this month to December 1st at the Jue Lin Vegetarian Restaurant on Wangping Street for his second solo calligraphy and engraving exhibition for five days. All items will be priced individually for sale. At the same time, he will also sell the second collection of Deng Fenweng's seal carvings. Weng has long been known as an eccentric genius in the literary world, with his artistry widely praised. It is expected that the exhibition will be a grand success.

Paris Cinema Premieres Cowlman's Masterpiece [The Thief] 192

Starting today (Wednesday), the Paris Cinema on Avenue Joffre will premiere the romantic blockbuster [The Thief]. [The Thief] was initially a famous novel popular worldwide, which then became a famous stage play known to American women and children. After the rise of sound films, United Artists of America turned the play into a sound film, starring the great actor Cowlman, who personally selected the charming star Keith Francis as his co-star. The combination of these two stars created a timeless masterpiece. The film was a sensation upon its release, gaining widespread acclaim.

Continued Compilation of Ciyuan to be Published on Schedule 193

The "Ciyuan" dictionary, published by the Commercial Press, has long occupied a solid and unshakable position among reference books in China. Due to recent domestic and international progress in various fields, many new items and concepts have emerged. The publishing house has undertaken the compilation of a "Ciyuan Continued Compilation," adding over two million words in content and enhancing the function of the original book to keep it up-to-date, meeting current needs. Since the pre-sale began, those who already own "Ciyuan" have taken advantage of the low-price opportunity to order in advance. The pre-sale deadline is at the end of this month, so orders are increasing daily. It is learned that the "Continued Compilation" will be published on schedule on December 1st, but due to shipping time, it may arrive slightly later in other cities.

Shanghai Tsinghua Alumni Welcome Mei Yi-chi 194

The new president of Tsinghua University arrived in Shanghai from the United States yesterday. Two to three hundred Tsinghua alumni in Shanghai will hold a banquet to welcome him at the Tsinghua Alumni Association at No. 50 Beijing Road on Thursday evening (November 26th) at 6 PM. President Mei has a long history with Tsinghua University, having served as the dean of academic affairs and acting president. Last year, he was appointed by the national government as the supervisor of Chinese students in the United States at Tsinghua. His return is expected to bring valuable contributions and achievements to the university.

Increased Postage for Southern Jiangxi Mail 195

According to the Shanghai Post Office, for parcels sent to various locations in southern Jiangxi, including Ganxian, Dagen, Tangjiangxu, Longnan, and Qunwu, which are the responsibility of the sender to forward via Guangdong, a surcharge will be collected from the recipient upon delivery due to high transportation costs.

New Style Razor and Blades of Gillett Goodwill 196

Over the past 28 years, the Gillette Company of the United States has sold countless Gillette safety razors. Based on years of experience, they have gradually improved and created the new and perfect Goodwill brand razors and blades. Shaving is smooth and close, providing an unprecedented experience. The company is currently operating day and night, producing 80,000 razors and 2.7 million blades per day to meet the demands of all parties. Vice President and General Manager Mr. Lu Hai plans to spend 2 million pounds next year on advertising in the world's most famous newspapers. The new Gillette razors and blades are priced low. The new blades can also be used on older razors. The new blades have four concave corners, so if they fall on the ground, the blades will remain straight, preventing cuts to the face during shaving. The new razor also does not need to be disassembled for cleaning. The blades will never rust. After shaving, loosen the frame, turn the four corners upright, rinse in water, and let it dry. The first batch of new goods has now arrived and is available at department stores and foreign goods stores.
